NOTICE

CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, Purushothaman, Biological son of R. Venkatarama Naidu, residing at No. 6, 6th Cross Street, Karpagam Gardens, Adyar,
Chennai-600 020. By way of this public notice in inform Thirumathi Kamalammal, wife of (Late) Narasimahalu Naidu has legally
adopted me as his son and 13th June 1988. By way a Registered deed on Document No. 108 of 13th June 1988. On the file
of the register of Thousand Lights, Chennai District. My adopted mother Thirumathi Kamalammal passed away
on 7th December 2004. Here after I shall be known as S.R. BABOO PURRSOTHAMAR.

Chennai,
24th June 2011.
